Third, we introduce automated evaluation methods for large language models to meet the high-reliability demands of legal retrieval scenarios. ### [223] [Compression Favors Consistency, Not Truth: When and Why Language Models Prefer Correct Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11749)
*Konstantin Krestnikov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究提出“压缩-一致性原理”，解释了语言模型为何在混合质量数据上训练时仍倾向于选择正确陈述，指出这是模型追求数据描述的简洁性和内部一致性的结果，而非内在的“真实性偏见”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究语言模型在包含错误信息的数据集上训练时，为何仍倾向于预测正确的陈述。

Method: 使用小规模（3.5M-86M 参数）GPT-2风格的字符级 Transformer 模型，在包含正确和错误规则的合成数学语料库上进行训练和测试。通过改变错误类型（随机错误 vs. 一致但错误的规则系统）以及引入嵌入式验证步骤和改变一致规则数量来验证模型行为。

Result: 在随机错误设置下，模型在配对评估中显著偏好正确补全，即使正确规则只占语料库的10%也能达到67.0%的准确率。当错误被替换为一致但错误的规则系统时，模型对正确性的偏好几乎消失。在更接近自然语言的合成世界中，该效应减弱但仍然存在（57.7%）。嵌入验证步骤可以恢复模型对正确性的偏好，而增加一致规则数量则能逐步提高准确率。

Conclusion: 模型表现出的“真实性偏见”主要是压缩压力和内部一致性偏好造成的副作用，而非模型本身具有追求真理的内在驱动力。

Abstract: Why do language models sometimes prefer correct statements even when trained on mixed-quality data? We introduce the Compression--Consistency Principle: next-token prediction favors hypotheses that allow shorter and more internally consistent descriptions of the training data. Truth bias emerges only when false alternatives are structurally harder to compress. We test this using small GPT-2-style character-level transformers (3.5M--86M parameters) on synthetic math corpora with controlled mixtures of correct and incorrect rules. In the random-error setting, models strongly prefer correct completions in paired evaluation: 83.1% accuracy at balanced data and 67.0% even when correct rules appear in only 10% of the corpus. Replacing random errors with a coherent but mathematically incorrect rule system largely eliminates the preference (near-chance accuracy). In a more natural-language-like synthetic world, the effect is weaker but still present (57.7%). Additional experiments show that embedding verification steps can restore preference for correctness even at small scale, while increasing the number of consistent rules produces a graded improvement in accuracy. Our results suggest that what appears as a "truth bias" is largely a side effect of compression pressure and preference for internal consistency, rather than an intrinsic drive toward truth. Full code and data are available at https://github.com/Rai220/compression-drives-truth.

</details>

The work outlines key aspects of disinformation, neural network architectures, and XAI techniques, with a focus on SHAP, LIME, and Integrated Gradients. In the experimental study, classification models were implemented and interpreted using these methods. The results show that XAI enhances model transparency and interpretability while maintaining high detection accuracy. Each method provides distinct explanatory value: SHAP offers detailed local attributions, LIME provides simple and intuitive explanations, and Integrated Gradients performs efficiently with convolutional models. The study also highlights limitations such as computational cost and sensitivity to parameterization. Overall, the findings demonstrate that integrating XAI with NLP is an effective approach to improving the reliability and trustworthiness of fake news detection systems.

### [225] [Large Language Models for Biomedical Article Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11780)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: This work presents a systematic and in-depth investigation of the utility of large language models as text classifiers for biomedical article classification. The study uses several small and mid-size open source models, as well as selected closed source ones, and is more comprehensive than most prior work with respect to the scope of evaluated configurations: different types of prompts, output processing methods for generating both class and class probability predictions, as well as few-shot example counts and selection methods. The performance of the most successful configurations is compared to that of conventional classification algorithms. The obtained average PR AUC over 15 challenging datasets above 0.4 for zero-shot prompting and nearly 0.5 for few-shot prompting comes close to that of the naïve Bayes classifier (0.5), the random forest algorithm (0.5 with default settings or 0.55 with hyperparameter tuning) and fine-tuned transformer models (0.5). These results confirm the utility of large language models as text classifiers for non-trivial domains and provide practical recommendations of the most promising setups, including in particular using output token probabilities for class probability prediction.

### [226] [DatedGPT: Preventing Lookahead Bias in Large Language Models with Time-Aware Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11838)
*Yutong Yan,Raphael Tang,Zhenyu Gao,Wenxi Jiang,Yao Lu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为DatedGPT的语言模型系列，通过在时间上划分的数据集上从头开始训练，以解决金融回测中大型语言模型的前视偏见问题，并验证了其知识的时效性。

Method: 开发了十二个1.3B参数的DatedGPT模型，每个模型从头开始训练，使用约1000亿个tokens，并严格按照2013年至2024年的年度时间界限进行数据划分。此外，通过通用领域和金融领域的数据集对模型进行指令微调，同样遵守时间界限。

Result: 基于困惑度（perplexity）的探测表明，每个模型的知识有效地被其数据截止年份所限制。在标准基准测试上的评估显示，DatedGPT模型在相似规模下具有与现有模型相当的性能。

Conclusion: DatedGPT模型有效地解决了大型语言模型在金融回测中的前视偏见问题，其知识的时效性得到了验证，并且在性能上具有竞争力。提供的交互式Web演示允许用户比较不同截止年份模型的响应。

Abstract: In financial backtesting, large language models pretrained on internet-scale data risk introducing lookahead bias that undermines their forecasting validity, as they may have already seen the true outcome during training. To address this, we present DatedGPT, a family of twelve 1.3B-parameter language models, each trained from scratch on approximately 100 billion tokens of temporally partitioned data with strict annual cutoffs spanning 2013 to 2024. We further enhance each model with instruction fine-tuning on both general-domain and finance-specific datasets curated to respect the same temporal boundaries. Perplexity-based probing confirms that each model's knowledge is effectively bounded by its data cutoff year, while evaluation on standard benchmarks shows competitive performance with existing models of similar scale. We provide an interactive web demo that allows users to query and compare responses from models across different cutoff years.

### [227] [Bielik-Minitron-7B: Compressing Large Language Models via Structured Pruning and Knowledge Distillation for the Polish Language](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11881)
*Remigiusz Kinas,Paweł Kiszczak,Sergio P. Perez,Krzysztof Ociepa,Łukasz Flis,Krzysztof Wróbel,Adrian Gwoździej*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究的动机是创建一种高效的语言模型，用于代表性不足的欧洲语言，同时降低部署成本。这需要减少模型大小和提高推理速度，同时尽量保留原始模型的性能。

Method: 该研究采用了两阶段压缩方法：首先，使用 NVIDIA Model Optimizer 进行结构化混合剪枝，然后使用 NVIDIA NeMo Framework 进行基于 Logit 的知识蒸馏。在压缩后，模型通过了监督微调 (SFT)、直接偏好优化 (DPO-P) 和强化学习 (GRPO) 的对齐流程。

Result: Bielik-Minitron-7B 的参数量从 11.04B 减少到 7.35B，减少了 33.4%。在保持性能方面，新模型恢复了基线模型约 90% 的性能。此外，推理速度提高了高达 50%。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了一种有效的途径，可以为代表性不足的语言创建语言模型，在降低推理部署成本的同时，保留原始模型的质量。这种压缩和对齐方法在性能和效率之间取得了良好的平衡。

Abstract: This report details the creation of Bielik-Minitron-7B, a compressed 7.35B parameter version of the Bielik-11B-v3.0 model, specifically optimized for European languages. By leveraging a two-stage compression methodology inspired by the NVIDIA Minitron approach, we combined structured hybrid pruning and knowledge distillation to reduce the model's parameter count by 33.4%, from 11.04B to 7.35B. We utilized the NVIDIA Model Optimizer for structural pruning and the NVIDIA NeMo Framework for logit-based distillation for quality recovery. Following distillation, the model underwent a rigorous alignment pipeline consisting of Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT), Direct Preference Optimization (DPO-P), and Reinforcement Learning (GRPO). Our final model successfully recovered approximately 90% of the baseline model's performance while providing up to 50% inference speedup. This approach demonstrates an efficient pathway to create language models for less-represented languages, preserving the original model quality while reducing inference deployment costs.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该框架采用后验温度缩放（post-hoc temperature scaling）、基于置信度的选择性预测（confidence-based selective prediction）和持续学习（continual learning）技术。具体而言，它只自动评分高置信度的预测，并将不确定的情况转交给人类评分员，同时通过持续学习适应不断变化的评分标准和新问题。

Conclusion: 不确定性量化对于实现可靠的AI辅助评分至关重要。CHiL(L)Grader通过将置信度估计整合到人工审核的工作流程中，实现了更安全、更可靠的自动化教育评估。

Instruction-tuned models tend to be overconfident, and their reliability deteriorates as curricula evolve, making fully autonomous deployment unsafe in high-stakes settings. We introduce CHiL(L)Grader, the first automated grading framework that incorporates calibrated confidence estimation into a human-in-the-loop workflow. Using post-hoc temperature scaling, confidence-based selective prediction, and continual learning, CHiL(L)Grader automates only high-confidence predictions while routing uncertain cases to human graders, and adapts to evolving rubrics and unseen questions. A QWK gap of 0.347 between accepted and rejected predictions confirms the effectiveness of the confidence-based routing. Each correction cycle strengthens the model's grading capability as it learns from teacher feedback. These results show that uncertainty quantification is key for reliable AI-assisted grading.

### [231] [BTZSC: A Benchmark for Zero-Shot Text Classification Across Cross-Encoders, Embedding Models, Rerankers and LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11991)
*Ilias Aarab*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了BTZSC基准测试，包含22个零样本文本分类数据集，用于系统比较NLI交叉编码器、嵌入模型、重排序器和指令微调LLM。结果显示，现代重排序器性能最佳，嵌入模型在准确率和延迟之间取得了良好平衡，LLM表现具有竞争力，而NLI交叉编码器性能停滞不前。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有零样本文本分类（ZSC）评估方法常常包含有监督的探测或微调，未能充分探索真正的零样本能力。研究者希望创建一个更全面的基准测试，以系统地比较不同ZSC模型家族的真实零样本性能。

Method: 作者构建了一个名为BTZSC的零样本文本分类基准测试，包含22个来自不同领域（情感、主题、意图、情绪）的数据集。他们使用该基准测试对四类模型进行了系统比较：NLI交叉编码器、嵌入模型、重排序器和指令微调LLM，共涉及38个模型检查点。

Result: 研究发现：1. 现代重排序器（如Qwen3-Reranker-8B）达到了新的SOTA（宏F1=0.72）。2. 强大的嵌入模型（如GTE-large-en-v1.5）显著缩小了准确率差距，并在准确率和延迟之间实现了最佳权衡。3. 指令微调LLM（4-12B参数）表现出竞争力（宏F1高达0.67），在主题分类上表现尤为突出，但落后于专门的重排序器。4. 随着骨干模型尺寸的增加，NLI交叉编码器的性能停滞不前。5. 扩展模型规模主要使重排序器和LLM受益，对嵌入模型的作用有限。

Conclusion: BTZSC是一个全面的零样本文本分类基准测试，通过系统比较揭示了不同模型家族的优劣。重排序器是当前零样本文本分类的最佳选择，嵌入模型提供了良好的准确率-延迟权衡，而LLM在特定任务上表现出色。研究结果为零样本文本理解领域的公平、可复现的研究提供了支持。

Abstract: Zero-shot text classification (ZSC) offers the promise of eliminating costly task-specific annotation by matching texts directly to human-readable label descriptions. While early approaches have predominantly relied on cross-encoder models fine-tuned for natural language inference (NLI), recent advances in text-embedding models, rerankers, and instruction-tuned large language models (LLMs) have challenged the dominance of NLI-based architectures. Yet, systematically comparing these diverse approaches remains difficult. Existing evaluations, such as MTEB, often incorporate labeled examples through supervised probes or fine-tuning, leaving genuine zero-shot capabilities underexplored. To address this, we introduce BTZSC, a comprehensive benchmark of 22 public datasets spanning sentiment, topic, intent, and emotion classification, capturing diverse domains, class cardinalities, and document lengths. Leveraging BTZSC, we conduct a systematic comparison across four major model families, NLI cross-encoders, embedding models, rerankers and instruction-tuned LLMs, encompassing 38 public and custom checkpoints. Our results show that: (i) modern rerankers, exemplified by Qwen3-Reranker-8B, set a new state-of-the-art with macro F1 = 0.72; (ii) strong embedding models such as GTE-large-en-v1.5 substantially close the accuracy gap while offering the best trade-off between accuracy and latency; (iii) instruction-tuned LLMs at 4--12B parameters achieve competitive performance (macro F1 up to 0.67), excelling particularly on topic classification but trailing specialized rerankers; (iv) NLI cross-encoders plateau even as backbone size increases; and (v) scaling primarily benefits rerankers and LLMs over embedding models. BTZSC and accompanying evaluation code are publicly released to support fair and reproducible progress in zero-shot text understanding.

### [232] [Just Use XML: Revisiting Joint Translation and Label Projection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12021)
*Thennal D K,Chris Biemann,Hans Ole Hatzel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为LabelPigeon的新框架，该框架通过XML标签联合进行机器翻译和标签投影，在跨语言迁移任务中取得了显著的改进，并且不会损害翻译质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有标签投影方法通常在机器翻译后单独执行，而一些尝试联合进行这两项任务的研究报告称翻译质量下降。因此，本文旨在重新评估这种说法，并开发一种能够同时进行翻译和标签投影的有效方法。

Method: 作者提出了LabelPigeon框架，该框架使用XML标签将翻译和标签投影联合起来。他们还设计了一个直接评估标签投影质量的方法，并在11种语言上评估了LabelPigeon的性能。此外，他们还在203种语言和不同标注复杂度下评估了翻译质量，并对27种语言的三个下游任务进行了跨语言迁移评估。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，使用XML标签的标签投影是一种有效且高效的标签迁移方法，它不会损害翻译质量，并且可以显著提高跨语言迁移任务的性能。

Abstract: Label projection is an effective technique for cross-lingual transfer, extending span-annotated datasets from a high-resource language to low-resource ones. Most approaches perform label projection as a separate step after machine translation, and prior work that combines the two reports degraded translation quality. We re-evaluate this claim with LabelPigeon, a novel framework that jointly performs translation and label projection via XML tags. We design a direct evaluation scheme for label projection, and find that LabelPigeon outperforms baselines and actively improves translation quality in 11 languages. We further assess translation quality across 203 languages and varying annotation complexity, finding consistent improvement attributed to additional fine-tuning. Finally, across 27 languages and three downstream tasks, we report substantial gains in cross-lingual transfer over comparable work, up to +39.9 F1 on NER. Overall, our results demonstrate that XML-tagged label projection provides effective and efficient label transfer without compromising translation quality.

### [233] [Translationese as a Rational Response to Translation Task Difficulty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12050)
*Maria Kunilovskaya*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出，翻译产生的系统性偏离（翻译腔）可以通过量化翻译任务的认知负荷来解释，并使用信息论指标和传统特征对英德语语料库进行了实证检验，发现翻译任务难度在一定程度上可以解释翻译腔，其中跨语言迁移难度比源文本复杂度更为重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管翻译腔（translationese）这一现象被广泛观察到，但目前缺乏一个统一的解释性理论。研究动机在于探究翻译腔是否源于翻译任务本身的认知负荷。

Method: 研究者将翻译腔操作化为由自动分类器生成的句子级翻译度得分，并将翻译任务难度概念化为源文本复杂度和跨语言迁移组成部分，主要通过基于大语言模型（LLM）的惊异度（surprisal）信息论指标进行量化，并辅以传统的句法和语义指标。研究使用了包含书面和口头子语料的双向英德语语料库。

Result: 结果表明，翻译腔可以在一定程度上由翻译任务难度解释，尤其是在英译德方向。在大多数实验中，跨语言迁移难度比源文本复杂度贡献更大。信息论指标在书面语模式下表现优于或持平于传统特征，但在口语模式下无优势。源文本的句法复杂度和翻译解决方案熵是跨语言对和语体中最强的翻译腔预测因子。

Conclusion: 翻译腔现象在一定程度上可以由翻译任务的认知负荷来解释，特别是跨语言迁移的难度。信息论指标在解释书面语翻译腔方面具有潜力，而源文本句法复杂度和翻译解决方案熵是关键的预测因子。

Abstract: Translations systematically diverge from texts originally produced in the target language, a phenomenon widely referred to as translationese. Translationese has been attributed to production tendencies (e.g. interference, simplification), socio-cultural variables, and language-pair effects, yet a unified explanatory account is still lacking. We propose that translationese reflects cognitive load inherent in the translation task itself. We test whether observable translationese can be predicted from quantifiable measures of translation task difficulty. Translationese is operationalised as a segment-level translatedness score produced by an automatic classifier. Translation task difficulty is conceptualised as comprising source-text and cross-lingual transfer components, operationalised mainly through information-theoretic metrics based on LLM surprisal, complemented by established syntactic and semantic alternatives. We use a bidirectional English-German corpus comprising written and spoken subcorpora. Results indicate that translationese can be partly explained by translation task difficulty, especially in English-to-German. For most experiments, cross-lingual transfer difficulty contributes more than source-text complexity. Information-theoretic indicators match or outperform traditional features in written mode, but offer no advantage in spoken mode. Source-text syntactic complexity and translation-solution entropy emerged as the strongest predictors of translationese across language pairs and modes.

</details>


### [234] [To Words and Beyond: Probing Large Language Models for Sentence-Level Psycholinguistic Norms of Memorability and Reading Times](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12105)
*Thomas Hikaru Clark,Carlos Arriaga,Javier Conde,Gonzalo Martínez,Pedro Reviriego*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLMs）经过微调后，可以有效预测句子记忆难度和阅读时间等句子级语言特征，且性能优于可解释的基线模型。然而，零样本和少样本提示LLMs进行此类预测的效果不稳定，提示在将LLM提示作为人类认知度量代理时需谨慎。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究LLMs能否应用于预测句子记忆难度和阅读时间等句子级语言特征，并与现有方法进行比较，以评估LLMs在理解和预测人类认知度量方面的潜力。

Method: 在LLMs上进行监督微调，以预测由人类数据生成的句子记忆难度和阅读时间得分。同时，评估了零样本和少样本提示LLMs的性能，并将其与可解释的基线预测器进行比较。

Result: 通过微调，LLMs能生成与人类数据高度相关的句子记忆难度和阅读时间得分，其预测能力优于基线模型。然而，零样本和少样本的提示性能表现不佳，结果不稳定。

Conclusion: LLMs在经过微调后，能够有效捕捉句子级语言特征的认知信息，但零样本和少样本提示方法的有效性尚待提高，提示在将LLM提示作为人类认知度量的代理时需要谨慎。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have recently been shown to produce estimates of psycholinguistic norms, such as valence, arousal, or concreteness, for words and multiword expressions, that correlate with human judgments. These estimates are obtained by prompting an LLM, in zero-shot fashion, with a question similar to those used in human studies. Meanwhile, for other norms such as lexical decision time or age of acquisition, LLMs require supervised fine-tuning to obtain results that align with ground-truth values. In this paper, we extend this approach to the previously unstudied features of sentence memorability and reading times, which involve the relationship between multiple words in a sentence-level context. Our results show that via fine-tuning, models can provide estimates that correlate with human-derived norms and exceed the predictive power of interpretable baseline predictors, demonstrating that LLMs contain useful information about sentence-level features. At the same time, our results show very mixed zero-shot and few-shot performance, providing further evidence that care is needed when using LLM-prompting as a proxy for human cognitive measures.

### [235] [SommBench: Assessing Sommelier Expertise of Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12117)
*William Brach,Tomas Bedej,Jacob Nielsen,Jacob Pichna,Juraj Bedej,Eemeli Saarensilta,Julie Dupouy,Gianluca Barmina,Andrea Blasi Núñez,Peter Schneider-Kamp,Kristian Košťál,Michal Ries,Lukas Galke Poech*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了SommBench，一个多语言的基准测试，用于评估大型语言模型在品酒师专业知识方面的能力，特别是它们能否通过文本描述理解和判断与嗅觉和味觉相关的感官属性。基准测试包含三个任务：葡萄酒理论问答、葡萄酒特征补全和食物-葡萄酒搭配，并提供多语言版本以区分语言能力和专业知识。研究发现，模型在理论问答方面表现良好，但在特征补全和食物-葡萄酒搭配方面面临挑战。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型在多语言和多文化能力方面取得快速进展，系统性地评估它们在这方面的能力变得越来越重要。现有的文化评估基准主要关注可以被语言编码的基本文化知识，而本文旨在探索语言模型是否能通过纯粹的文本描述来掌握如嗅觉和味觉般高度依赖感官的专业领域知识，具体以品酒师专业知识为例。

Result: 在评估中，最先进的模型在葡萄酒理论问答任务上表现出色，其中一个闭源模型达到了97%的准确率。然而，在葡萄酒特征补全任务上，模型的表现（最高65%）和食物-葡萄酒搭配任务（MCC介于0到0.39之间）则显示出更大的挑战性。

Conclusion: SommBench是一个有价值且具有挑战性的基准测试，可以有效评估大型语言模型在品酒师专业知识方面的能力，特别是它们通过文本描述理解感官属性的能力。现有模型在理论知识问答方面表现良好，但在更依赖感官判断的特征补全和食物-葡萄酒搭配方面仍有很大的提升空间。

Abstract: With the rapid advances of large language models, it becomes increasingly important to systematically evaluate their multilingual and multicultural capabilities. Previous cultural evaluation benchmarks focus mainly on basic cultural knowledge that can be encoded in linguistic form. Here, we propose SommBench, a multilingual benchmark to assess sommelier expertise, a domain deeply grounded in the senses of smell and taste. While language models learn about sensory properties exclusively through textual descriptions, SommBench tests whether this textual grounding is sufficient to emulate expert-level sensory judgment. SommBench comprises three main tasks: Wine Theory Question Answering (WTQA), Wine Feature Completion (WFC), and Food-Wine Pairing (FWP). SommBench is available in multiple languages: English, Slovak, Swedish, Finnish, German, Danish, Italian, and Spanish. This helps separate a language model's wine expertise from its language skills. The benchmark datasets were developed in close collaboration with a professional sommelier and native speakers of the respective languages, resulting in 1,024 wine theory question-answering questions, 1,000 wine feature-completion examples, and 1,000 food-wine pairing examples. We provide results for the most popular language models, including closed-weights models such as Gemini 2.5, and open-weights models, such as GPT-OSS and Qwen 3. Our results show that the most capable models perform well on wine theory question answering (up to 97% correct with a closed-weights model), yet feature completion (peaking at 65%) and food-wine pairing show (MCC ranging between 0 and 0.39) turn out to be more challenging. These results position SommBench as an interesting and challenging benchmark for evaluating the sommelier expertise of language models. The benchmark is publicly available at https://github.com/sommify/sommbench.

### [236] [Cross-Context Review: Improving LLM Output Quality by Separating Production and Review Sessions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12123)
*Tae-Eun Song*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为跨上下文审查（CCR）的新方法，该方法通过在与生成过程隔离的新会话中进行审查，显著提高了大型语言模型发现自身错误的效率，优于同一会话内审查（SR）、重复审查（SR2）和上下文感知子代理审查（SA）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在同一会话中难以发现自身输出的错误。

Method: 提出了一种跨上下文审查（CCR）方法，即在一个全新的、不访问生产对话历史的会话中进行审查。通过实验比较了四种审查条件：同一会话自我审查（SR）、重复自我审查（SR2）、上下文感知子代理审查（SA）和跨上下文审查（CCR）。

Result: CCR 在 30 个包含 150 个错误的人工制品测试中，F1 值为 28.6%，显著优于 SR（24.6%）、SR2（21.7%）和 SA（23.8%）。重复审查（SR2）并未比单次审查（SR）有显著优势，表明 CCR 的优势源于上下文分离。

Conclusion: 跨上下文审查（CCR）是一种简单有效的方法，能够显著提高大型语言模型发现自身错误的能力，且无需额外基础设施，仅需一个额外的会话。

Abstract: Large language models struggle to catch errors in their own outputs when the review happens in the same session that produced them. This paper introduces Cross-Context Review (CCR), a straightforward method where the review is conducted in a fresh session with no access to the production conversation history. We ran a controlled experiment: 30 artifacts (code, technical documents, presentation scripts) with 150 injected errors, tested under four review conditions -- same-session Self-Review (SR), repeated Self-Review (SR2), context-aware Subagent Review (SA), and Cross-Context Review (CCR). Over 360 reviews, CCR reached an F1 of 28.6%, outperforming SR (24.6%, p=0.008, d=0.52), SR2 (21.7%, p<0.001, d=0.72), and SA (23.8%, p=0.004, d=0.57). The SR2 result matters most for interpretation: reviewing twice in the same session did not beat reviewing once (p=0.11), which rules out repetition as an explanation for CCR's advantage. The benefit comes from context separation itself. CCR works with any model, needs no infrastructure, and costs only one extra session.

Using this framework, we show that while the best agents can match human searchers in raw accuracy, they succeed on largely different questions and rely on brute-force search to compensate for weak strategic planning. They fail to close the nearly 20% gap to oracle performance, persisting in unproductive loops. We release the dataset and evaluation harness to help facilitate the transition from brute-force retrieval to calibrated, efficient reasoning.

### [239] [QAQ: Bidirectional Semantic Coherence for Selecting High-Quality Synthetic Code Instructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12165)
*Jiayin Lei,Ming Ma,Yunxi Duan,Chenxi Li,Tianming Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为QAQ的新型合成数据选择框架，通过评估答案对查询的预测能力（Q|A）来衡量数据质量，而非现有方法关注的查询对答案的预测能力（A|Q）。QAQ利用反向互信息（RMI）来量化答案提供查询信息的能力，发现低RMI和过高的RMI都表明数据质量问题。结合强弱模型的不一致性，QAQ能有效筛选出有效且具有挑战性的数据。在WarriorCoder数据集上的实验表明，QAQ在只使用25%数据的情况下，性能可与全数据训练媲美，并显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有合成数据选择方法（如IFD）主要关注模型生成答案的能力（A|Q），但在处理包含噪声和幻觉的合成数据时存在歧义，难以区分任务本身的难度和模型产生的幻觉。因此，需要一种新的方法来更有效地评估合成数据的质量。

Method: 提出QAQ框架，从反向角度评估数据质量，即评估答案对查询的预测能力（Q|A）。定义反向互信息（RMI）来量化答案提供查询信息的增益。RMI的极值（过低或过高）都表明数据质量问题。结合强弱模型的预测不一致性，设计数据选择策略。

Result: 实验表明，QAQ框架通过反向互信息（RMI）和强弱模型的不一致性，能够有效识别高质量的合成数据。在WarriorCoder数据集上，使用QAQ选择25%的数据进行训练，性能与使用全部数据训练相当，并显著优于现有的数据选择方法。

Conclusion: 双向语义一致性对于合成数据质量至关重要。QAQ框架通过评估答案对查询的预测能力，并结合模型不一致性，提供了一种有效且可扩展的数据选择方法，能够降低计算成本，同时保持模型性能。

Abstract: Synthetic data has become essential for training code generation models, yet it introduces significant noise and hallucinations that are difficult to detect with current metrics. Existing data selection methods like Instruction-Following Difficulty (IFD) typically assess how hard a model generates an answer given a query ($A|Q$). However, this metric is ambiguous on noisy synthetic data, where low probability can distinguish between intrinsic task complexity and model-generated hallucinations. Here, we propose QAQ, a novel data selection framework that evaluates data quality from the reverse direction: how well can the answer predict the query ($Q|A$)? We define Reverse Mutual Information (RMI) to quantify the information gain about the query conditioned on the answer. Our analyses reveal that both extremes of RMI signal quality issues: low RMI indicates semantic misalignment, while excessively high RMI may contain defect patterns that LLMs easily recognize. Furthermore, we introduce a selection strategy based on the disagreement between strong and weak models to identify samples that are valid yet challenging. Experiments on the WarriorCoder dataset demonstrate that selecting just 25% of data using stratified RMI achieves comparable performance to full-data training, significantly outperforming existing data selection methods. Our approach highlights the importance of bidirectional semantic coherence in synthetic data curation, offering a scalable pathway to reduce computational costs without sacrificing model capability.

Furthermore, we propose compressed model variants trained via knowledge distillation. ### [241] [IndexCache: Accelerating Sparse Attention via Cross-Layer Index Reuse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12201)
*Yushi Bai,Qian Dong,Ting Jiang,Xin Lv,Zhengxiao Du,Aohan Zeng,Jie Tang,Juanzi Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出IndexCache，一种通过在连续层之间共享稀疏注意力索引来优化DeepSeek Sparse Attention (DSA)的方法，将索引器计算量减少75%，同时保持模型性能，并实现预填充和解码速度的大幅提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有DSA方法虽然有效，但其索引器仍存在$O(L^2)$的计算复杂度，且每层都需要独立运行，造成冗余，尤其是在连续层索引高度相似的情况下。

Method: IndexCache将模型层划分为“Full”层（运行索引器）和“Shared”层（复用最近“Full”层的索引）。提出了两种方法来确定和优化层配置：1. 训练无关的IndexCache使用贪婪搜索算法最小化语言模型损失；2. 训练感知的IndexCache引入多层蒸馏损失，使每个索引器学习服务层级的平均注意力分布。

Result: 在30B DSA模型上，IndexCache可移除75%的索引器计算量，模型质量几乎无损，预填充速度提升高达1.82倍，解码速度提升1.48倍。在GLM-5模型上也验证了有效性。

Conclusion: IndexCache通过有效利用跨层冗余，显著提高了稀疏注意力机制的效率，为长上下文大模型带来了更快的推理速度和更低的成本，且易于集成到现有模型中。

Abstract: Long-context agentic workflows have emerged as a defining use case for large language models, making attention efficiency critical for both inference speed and serving cost. Sparse attention addresses this challenge effectively, and DeepSeek Sparse Attention (DSA) is a representative production-grade solution: a lightweight lightning indexer selects the top-k most relevant tokens per query, reducing core attention from $O(L^2)$ to $O(Lk)$. However, the indexer itself retains $O(L^2)$ complexity and must run independently at every layer, despite the fact that the resulting top-k selections are highly similar across consecutive layers. We present IndexCache, which exploits this cross-layer redundancy by partitioning layers into a small set of Full layers that run their own indexers and a majority of Shared layers that simply reuse the nearest Full layer's top-k indices. We propose two complementary approaches to determine and optimize this configuration. Training-free IndexCache applies a greedy search algorithm that selects which layers to retain indexers by directly minimizing language modeling loss on a calibration set, requiring no weight updates. Training-aware IndexCache introduces a multi-layer distillation loss that trains each retained indexer against the averaged attention distributions of all layers it serves, enabling even simple interleaved patterns to match full-indexer accuracy. Experimental results on a 30B DSA model show that IndexCache can remove 75% of indexer computations with negligible quality degradation, achieving up to 1.82$\times$ prefill speedup and 1.48$\times$ decode speedup compared to standard DSA. These positive results are further confirmed by our preliminary experiments on the production-scale GLM-5 model (Figure 1).

</details>


### [242] [CLASP: Defending Hybrid Large Language Models Against Hidden State Poisoning Attacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12206)
*Alexandre Le Mercier,Thomas Demeester,Chris Develder*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为 CLASP 的模型，用于防御针对状态空间模型（SSMs）的隐藏状态中毒攻击（HiSPAs）。CLASP 通过分析 Mamba 模型输出嵌入中的模式，并利用 XGBoost 分类器识别恶意 token，实现了高效且准确的攻击检测，并且能够泛化到未见的攻击模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Mamba 等 SSMs 作为 Transformer 的高效替代品获得了广泛关注，但其隐藏状态中毒攻击（HiSPA）的漏洞对其安全构成了严重威胁。因此，开发一种有效的 HiSPA 防御机制至关重要。

Method: 研究将 HiSPA 缓解问题构建为一个 token 级别的二元分类任务。CLASP 利用 Mamba 的块输出嵌入（BOEs）中的独特模式，并使用 XGBoost 分类器来识别恶意 token，从而以最小的计算开销进行防御。实验在筛选简历的真实场景中进行。

Result: 在 2,483 份简历（共 9.5M token）的语料库上，CLASP 在恶意 token 检测方面达到了 95.9% 的 token 级别 F1 分数和 99.3% 的文档级别 F1 分数。模型对未见的攻击模式表现出良好的泛化能力，在留一法交叉验证中达到 96.9% 的文档级别 F1 分数，在结构新颖的触发器聚类交叉验证中保持了 91.6% 的平均文档级别 F1 分数。CLASP 的运行独立于任何下游模型，处理速度可达 1,032 token/秒，VRAM 消耗低于 4GB。

Conclusion: CLASP 是一种高效且准确的 HiSPA 防御模型，能够识别恶意 token 并具有良好的泛化能力。其低计算开销和独立性使其适合作为 SSMs 和混合架构的轻量级前线防御部署。

Abstract: State space models (SSMs) like Mamba have gained significant traction as efficient alternatives to Transformers, achieving linear complexity while maintaining competitive performance. However, Hidden State Poisoning Attacks (HiSPAs), a recently discovered vulnerability that corrupts SSM memory through adversarial strings, pose a critical threat to these architectures and their hybrid variants. Framing the HiSPA mitigation task as a binary classification problem at the token level, we introduce the CLASP model to defend against this threat. CLASP exploits distinct patterns in Mamba's block output embeddings (BOEs) and uses an XGBoost classifier to identify malicious tokens with minimal computational overhead. We consider a realistic scenario in which both SSMs and HiSPAs are likely to be used: an LLM screening résumés to identify the best candidates for a role. Evaluated on a corpus of 2,483 résumés totaling 9.5M tokens with controlled injections, CLASP achieves 95.9% token-level F1 score and 99.3% document-level F1 score on malicious tokens detection. Crucially, the model generalizes to unseen attack patterns: under leave-one-out cross-validation, performance remains high (96.9% document-level F1), while under clustered cross-validation with structurally novel triggers, it maintains useful detection capability (91.6% average document-level F1). Operating independently of any downstream model, CLASP processes 1,032 tokens per second with under 4GB VRAM consumption, potentially making it suitable for real-world deployment as a lightweight front-line defense for SSM-based and hybrid architectures. All code and detailed results are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/hispikes-91C0.

</details>


### [243] [Sparking Scientific Creativity via LLM-Driven Interdisciplinary Inspiration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12226)
*Priyanka Kargupta,Shuhaib Mehri,Dilek Hakkani-Tur,Jiawei Han*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Idea-Catalyst 是一个新颖的框架，它通过识别跨学科见解来支持人类和大型语言模型进行创造性推理，从而提高研究的新颖性和深刻性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前学术研究尽管有跨学科合作的潜力，但仍局限于单一领域。现有的AI驱动的科学发现方法侧重于快速实验设计，忽视了创造性跨学科突破的关键探索性、协作式推理过程。因此，prior efforts 侧重于自动化科学发现，而非增强科学颠覆背后的推理过程。

Method: Idea-Catalyst 从抽象的研究目标出发，通过以下方式辅助头脑风暴：1. 定义和评估研究目标；2. 认识到某一领域的机遇和未解决的挑战；3. 基于潜在影响策略性地探索跨学科思想。具体来说，它将抽象目标分解为核心目标研究问题，分析进展和开放挑战，并将这些挑战重构为领域无关的概念问题，以便从其他学科检索类似问题。最后，它通过综合和重新背景化来自这些领域的新见解，并根据跨学科潜力对源领域进行排名。

Result: 与现有方法相比，Idea-Catalyst 能够提高平均新颖性 21%，深刻性 16%，同时保持与原始研究问题的关联性。

Conclusion: Idea-Catalyst 框架通过系统地识别跨学科见解，有效地支持了人类和大型语言模型进行创造性推理，从而在保持研究目标的同时，提高了研究的创新性和洞察力。

Abstract: Despite interdisciplinary research leading to larger and longer-term impact, most work remains confined to single-domain academic silos. Recent AI-based approaches to scientific discovery show promise for interdisciplinary research, but many prioritize rapidly designing experiments and solutions, bypassing the exploratory, collaborative reasoning processes that drive creative interdisciplinary breakthroughs. As a result, prior efforts largely prioritize automating scientific discovery rather than augmenting the reasoning processes that underlie scientific disruption. We present Idea-Catalyst, a novel framework that systematically identifies interdisciplinary insights to support creative reasoning in both humans and large language models. Starting from an abstract research goal, Idea-Catalyst is designed to assist the brainstorming stage, explicitly avoiding premature anchoring on specific solutions. The framework embodies key metacognitive features of interdisciplinary reasoning: (a) defining and assessing research goals, (b) awareness of a domain's opportunities and unresolved challenges, and (c) strategic exploration of interdisciplinary ideas based on impact potential. Concretely, Idea-Catalyst decomposes an abstract goal (e.g., improving human-AI collaboration) into core target-domain research questions that guide the analysis of progress and open challenges within that domain. These challenges are reformulated as domain-agnostic conceptual problems, enabling retrieval from external disciplines (e.g., Psychology, Sociology) that address analogous issues. By synthesizing and recontextualizing insights from these domains back into the target domain, Idea-Catalyst ranks source domains by their interdisciplinary potential. Empirically, this targeted integration improves average novelty by 21% and insightfulness by 16%, while remaining grounded in the original research problem.

</details>


### [244] [SciMDR: Benchmarking and Advancing Scientific Multimodal Document Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12249)
*Ziyu Chen,Yilun Zhao,Chengye Wang,Rilyn Han,Manasi Patwardhan,Arman Cohan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为synthesize-and-reground的两阶段框架，用于构建大规模、真实且忠实的科学多模态文档推理数据集SciMDR，并辅以评估基准SciMDR-Eval。在SciMDR上微调的模型在需要复杂文档级推理的任务上表现出显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建用于基础模型训练的科学多模态文档推理数据集，在规模、忠实性和真实性之间存在固有的权衡。为了解决这一挑战，需要一个能够同时兼顾这三个方面的数据集构建方法。

Method: 该研究提出了一个名为synthesize-and-reground的两阶段框架。第一阶段是Claim-Centric QA Synthesis，用于生成忠实、独立的问答对和基于聚焦片段的推理。第二阶段是Document-Scale Regrounding，用于将这些问答对以编程方式重新嵌入到全文档任务中，以确保真实性。基于此框架，研究人员构建了SciMDR数据集，包含300K问答对和推理链，以及SciMDR-Eval评估基准。

Result: 在SciMDR上微调的模型在多个科学问答基准上取得了显著的改进，尤其是在需要复杂文档级推理的任务上。

Conclusion: synthesize-and-reground框架能够有效地构建大规模、忠实且真实的科学多模态文档推理数据集。在SciMDR上进行微调可以显著提升模型在科学问答任务中的表现，特别是那些需要理解复杂文档结构的推理任务。

Abstract: Constructing scientific multimodal document reasoning datasets for foundation model training involves an inherent trade-off among scale, faithfulness, and realism. To address this challenge, we introduce the synthesize-and-reground framework, a two-stage pipeline comprising: (1) Claim-Centric QA Synthesis, which generates faithful, isolated QA pairs and reasoning on focused segments, and (2) Document-Scale Regrounding, which programmatically re-embeds these pairs into full-document tasks to ensure realistic complexity. Using this framework, we construct SciMDR, a large-scale training dataset for cross-modal comprehension, comprising 300K QA pairs with explicit reasoning chains across 20K scientific papers. We further construct SciMDR-Eval, an expert-annotated benchmark to evaluate multimodal comprehension within full-length scientific workflows. Experiments demonstrate that models fine-tuned on SciMDR achieve significant improvements across multiple scientific QA benchmarks, particularly in those tasks requiring complex document-level reasoning.

</details>

### [245] [TinyNav: End-to-End TinyML for Real-Time Autonomous Navigation on Microcontrollers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11071)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用ESP32微控制器，训练一个量化的2D卷积神经网络（23k参数），处理20帧的深度数据滑动窗口，预测转向和油门指令，避免使用3D卷积和循环层，实现30毫秒的推理延迟。

Result: TinyNav系统在ESP32上实现了30毫秒的推理延迟，并通过相关性分析和Grad-CAM验证了其空间感知和避障能力。

Abstract: Autonomous navigation typically relies on power-intensive processors, limiting accessibility in low-cost robotics. Although microcontrollers offer a resource-efficient alternative, they impose strict constraints on model complexity. We present TinyNav, an end-to-end TinyML system for real-time autonomous navigation on an ESP32 microcontroller. A custom-trained, quantized 2D convolutional neural network processes a 20-frame sliding window of depth data to predict steering and throttle commands. By avoiding 3D convolutions and recurrent layers, the 23k-parameter model achieves 30 ms inference latency. Correlation analysis and Grad-CAM validation indicate consistent spatial awareness and obstacle avoidance behavior. TinyNav demonstrates that responsive autonomous control can be deployed directly on highly constrained edge devices, reducing reliance on external compute resources.

### [246] [OA-NBV: Occlusion-Aware Next-Best-View Planning for Human-Centered Active Perception on Mobile Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11072)
*Boxun Hu,Chang Chang,Jiawei Ge,Man Namgung,Xiaomin Lin,Axel Krieger,Tinoosh Mohsenin*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为OA-NBV（Occlusion-Aware Next-Best-View Planning for Human-Centered Active Perception on Mobile Robots）的遮挡感知方法，使移动机器人能够自主选择最佳的下一个观察点，以获得被部分遮挡的人体的更完整视图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人导航方法在处理遮挡和获得清晰目标视图方面存在不足，尤其是在搜索、分诊和灾难响应等以人为中心的操作中，这限制了机器人在复杂环境中的感知能力。因此，需要一种能够解决遮挡问题并专注于立即获得可用观察结果的视角选择方法。

Method: OA-NBV是一个集成感知和运动规划的流水线。它通过一个以目标为中心的可见性模型来评估候选视点，该模型考虑了遮挡、目标尺度和目标完整性。同时，它将候选视点限制在机器人可行的姿态范围内。

Result: OA-NBV在模拟和真实世界试验中均实现了超过90%的成功率。与基线NBV方法相比，OA-NBV在遮挡情况下性能没有明显下降，并且显著提高了观察质量，包括目标区域的归一化面积增加至少81%，关键点可见性增加至少58%。

Conclusion: OA-NBV是一种有效的遮挡感知方法，可以显著改善移动机器人在处理部分遮挡的人体时的观察能力，并可作为各种以人为中心的下游任务的即插即用型视图选择模块。

Abstract: We naturally step sideways or lean to see around the obstacle when our view is blocked, and recover a more informative observation. Enabling robots to make the same kind of viewpoint choice is critical for human-centered operations, including search, triage, and disaster response, where cluttered environments and partial visibility frequently degrade downstream perception. However, many Next-Best-View (NBV) methods primarily optimize generic exploration or long-horizon coverage, and do not explicitly target the immediate goal of obtaining a single usable observation of a partially occluded person under real motion constraints. We present Occlusion-Aware Next-Best-View Planning for Human-Centered Active Perception on Mobile Robots (OA-NBV), an occlusion-aware NBV pipeline that autonomously selects the next traversable viewpoint to obtain a more complete view of an occluded human. OA-NBV integrates perception and motion planning by scoring candidate viewpoints using a target-centric visibility model that accounts for occlusion, target scale, and target completeness, while restricting candidates to feasible robot poses. OA-NBV achieves over 90% success rate in both simulation and real-world trials, while baseline NBV methods degrade sharply under occlusion. Beyond success rate, OA-NBV improves observation quality: compared to the strongest baseline, it increases normalized target area by at least 81% and keypoint visibility by at least 58% across settings, making it a drop-in view-selection module for diverse human-centered downstream tasks.

</details>


### [247] [DRAFTO: Decoupled Reduced-space and Adaptive Feasibility-repair Trajectory Optimization for Robotic Manipulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11074)
*Yichang Feng,Xiao Liang,Minghui Zheng*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为DRAFTO的新型轨迹优化算法，该算法通过解耦和自适应可行性修复来提高效率和可靠性，并在多种基准测试和复杂操作任务中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了提高轨迹优化算法的效率和可靠性，特别是在处理关节限制和保证可行性方面。

Method: DRAFTO算法通过构建包含平滑度、安全性、关节限制和任务要求的约束目标，并优化轨迹参数化中的基函数系数。它将优化过程解耦为低维空间中的高斯-牛顿下降和用于初始化及末端可行性修复的约束二次规划。该算法还采用了具有非单调策略的两阶段接受规则以及 hinge-squared 惩罚项来处理不等式约束，以保证全局收敛性。

Result: DRAFTO算法在与CHOMP、TrajOpt、GPMP2、FACTO等基于优化的规划器以及RRT-Connect、RRT*、PRM等基于采样的规划器的基准测试中，展现出高效性和可靠性。此外，在抓取抽屉中物体的实验中，也证明了其在复杂操作任务中的应用潜力。

Conclusion: DRAFTO算法是一种高效且可靠的轨迹优化方法，能够处理复杂的约束条件，并在各种场景下表现出色，有望应用于更复杂的机器人操作任务。

Abstract: This paper introduces a new algorithm for trajectory optimization, Decoupled Reduced-space and Adaptive Feasibility-repair Trajectory Optimization (DRAFTO). It first constructs a constrained objective that accounts for smoothness, safety, joint limits, and task requirements. Then, it optimizes the coefficients, which are the coordinates of a set of basis functions for trajectory parameterization. To reduce the number of repeated constrained optimizations while handling joint-limit feasibility, the optimization is decoupled into a reduced-space Gauss-Newton (GN) descent for the main iterations and constrained quadratic programming for initialization and terminal feasibility repair. The two-phase acceptance rule with a non-monotone policy is applied to the GN model, which uses a hinge-squared penalty for inequality constraints, to ensure globalizability. The results of our benchmark tests against optimization-based planners, such as CHOMP, TrajOpt, GPMP2, and FACTO, and sampling-based planners, such as RRT-Connect, RRT*, and PRM, validate the high efficiency and reliability across diverse scenarios and tasks. The experiment involving grabbing an object from a drawer further demonstrates the potential for implementation in complex manipulation tasks. The supplemental video is available at https://youtu.be/XisFI37YyTQ.

</details>

All these factors restrict the practical deployment of current robotic disassembly systems and leave them highly reliant on human labor. With the recent development of foundation models in robotics, vision-language-action (VLA) models have shown impressive performance on standard robotic manipulation tasks, but their applicability to complex, contact-rich, and long-horizon industrial practices like disassembly, which requires sequential and precise manipulation, remains limited. To address this challenge, we propose SELF-VLA, an agentic VLA framework that integrates explicit disassembly skills. Experimental studies demonstrate that our framework significantly outperforms current state-of-the-art end-to-end VLA models on two contact-rich disassembly tasks. ### [249] [TATIC: Task-Aware Temporal Learning for Human Intent Inference from Physical Corrections in Human-Robot Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11077)
*Jiurun Song,Xiao Liang,Minghui Zheng*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为TATIC的统一框架，结合接触力估计和时间卷积网络（TCN），能够从短暂的物理交互中同时推断离散的任务级别意图和估计连续的运动级别参数，以实现人机协作中的在线适应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的人机协作（HRC）系统难以从物理纠正中提取任务级别的语义意图，而现有的基于基础模型的方法主要依赖视觉和语言输入，缺乏解释物理反馈的机制。同时，传统的物理人机交互（pHRI）方法虽然利用物理纠正进行轨迹引导，但在推断任务级别语义方面存在困难。

Method: 提出TATIC框架，利用基于扭矩的接触力估计和任务感知的Temporal Convolutional Network（TCN）。通过任务对齐特征规范化确保鲁棒性，并采用意图驱动的自适应方案将推断出的意图转化为机器人运动的适应。

Result: 在任务意图识别方面取得了0.904的Macro-F1分数，并在协作拆卸任务中成功进行了硬件验证。

Conclusion: TATIC框架能够有效地从短暂的物理纠正中同时推断任务级别意图和估计运动级别参数，从而在动态和演变的人机协作场景中实现机器人对人类意图的鲁棒适应。

Abstract: In human-robot collaboration (HRC), robots must adapt online to dynamic task constraints and evolving human intent. While physical corrections provide a natural, low-latency channel for operators to convey motion-level adjustments, extracting task-level semantic intent from such brief interactions remains challenging. Existing foundation-model-based approaches primarily rely on vision and language inputs and lack mechanisms to interpret physical feedback. Meanwhile, traditional physical human-robot interaction (pHRI) methods leverage physical corrections for trajectory guidance but struggle to infer task-level semantics. To bridge this gap, we propose TATIC, a unified framework that utilizes torque-based contact force estimation and a task-aware Temporal Convolutional Network (TCN) to jointly infer discrete task-level intent and estimate continuous motion-level parameters from brief physical corrections. Task-aligned feature canonicalization ensures robust generalization across diverse layouts, while an intent-driven adaptation scheme translates inferred human intent into robot motion adaptations. Experiments achieve a 0.904 Macro-F1 score in intent recognition and demonstrate successful hardware validation in collaborative disassembly (see experimental video at https://youtu.be/xF8A52qwEc8).

### [250] [Edge-Assisted Multi-Robot Visual-Inertial SLAM with Efficient Communication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11085)
*Xin Liu,Shuhuan Wen,Jing Zhao,Tony Z. Qiu,Hong Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于光流跟踪和金字塔IMU预测的轻量级SLAM方法，并结合机器人-边缘-云分层架构，实现了实时多机器人协同SLAM，在保证低计算负载的同时，提高了定位精度和带宽效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决单机器人SLAM受限于计算、通信和存储能力，以及多机器人SLAM在云端协作时面临带宽限制和通信延迟导致的性能下降问题。

Method: 提出了一种基于光流跟踪的金字塔IMU预测轻量级SLAM方法；设计了一种机器人-边缘-云分层架构的集中式多机器人SLAM系统；采用特征点和关键帧描述符的无损编码和压缩技术进行数据传输。

Result: 在EuRoC数据集上验证，与现有的局部特征压缩方法相比，传输数据量更少；与现有集中式多机器人SLAM方案相比，在低计算负载下实现了相同或更好的定位精度。

Conclusion: 所提出的轻量级SLAM方法和机器人-边缘-云协同架构能够有效降低计算成本和带宽占用，实现实时、高精度的多机器人协同SLAM。

Abstract: The integration of cloud computing and edge computing is an effective way to achieve global consistent and real-time multi-robot Simultaneous Localization and Mapping (SLAM). Cloud computing effectively solves the problem of limited computing, communication and storage capacity of terminal equipment. However, limited bandwidth and extremely long communication links between terminal devices and the cloud result in serious performance degradation of multi-robot SLAM systems. To reduce the computational cost of feature tracking and improve the real-time performance of the robot, a lightweight SLAM method of optical flow tracking based on pyramid IMU prediction is proposed. On this basis, a centralized multi-robot SLAM system based on a robot-edge-cloud layered architecture is proposed to realize real-time collaborative SLAM. It avoids the problems of limited on-board computing resources and low execution efficiency of single robot. In this framework, only the feature points and keyframe descriptors are transmitted and lossless encoding and compression are carried out to realize real-time remote information transmission with limited bandwidth resources. This design reduces the actual bandwidth occupied in the process of data transmission, and does not cause the loss of SLAM accuracy caused by data compression. Through experimental verification on the EuRoC dataset, compared with the current most advanced local feature compression method, our method can achieve lower data volume feature transmission, and compared with the current advanced centralized multi-robot SLAM scheme, it can achieve the same or better positioning accuracy under low computational load.

</details>

In terms of training, for the GR00T-N1.5 model, utilizing thousand-GPU clusters and data at the scale of hundreds of millions, the single-round training time has been reduced from 15 hours to just 22 minutes, achieving a 40-fold speedup. At the model layer, by combining variable-length FlashAttention and Data Packing, we have moved from sample redundancy to sequence integration, resulting in a 188% speed increase; π-0.5 attention optimization has accelerated training by 165%; and FP8 quantization has delivered a 140% speedup. ### [252] [ResWM: Residual-Action World Model for Visual RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11110)
*Jseen Zhang,Gabriel Adineera,Jinzhou Tan,Jinoh Kim*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为残差动作世界模型（ResWM）的新框架，通过将绝对动作改为残差动作，显著提高了强化学习在机器人和连续控制任务中的稳定性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的基于模型的强化学习方法直接依赖绝对动作进行预测，导致优化不稳定，尤其是在机器人和连续控制任务中。这是因为最优动作的分布是任务依赖且未知的，容易导致振荡或低效控制。

Method: ResWM将控制变量从绝对动作重构为相对于前一步的增量调整（残差动作）。此外，提出了一种观测差分编码器，显式地对相邻帧的变化进行建模，生成与残差动作耦合的紧凑潜在动力学。该框架整合到Dreamer风格的潜在动力学模型中，并在残差动作空间中进行想象回滚和策略优化。

Result: 在DeepMind Control Suite上的实验结果表明，ResWM在样本效率、渐进回报和控制平滑度方面均取得了持续的改进，显著优于Dreamer和TD-MPC等基线方法。ResWM产生的动作轨迹更稳定、能耗更低。

Conclusion: ResWM通过将动作建模为残差，提供了一种简单而强大的方法，有效缓解了传统模型优化中的不稳定性问题，为机器人实际应用中的强化学习提供了更稳定、更节能的解决方案。

Abstract: Learning predictive world models from raw visual observations is a central challenge in reinforcement learning (RL), especially for robotics and continuous control. Conventional model-based RL frameworks directly condition future predictions on absolute actions, which makes optimization unstable: the optimal action distributions are task-dependent, unknown a priori, and often lead to oscillatory or inefficient control. To address this, we introduce the Residual-Action World Model (ResWM), a new framework that reformulates the control variable from absolute actions to residual actions -- incremental adjustments relative to the previous step. This design aligns with the inherent smoothness of real-world control, reduces the effective search space, and stabilizes long-horizon planning. To further strengthen the representation, we propose an Observation Difference Encoder that explicitly models the changes between adjacent frames, yielding compact latent dynamics that are naturally coupled with residual actions. ResWM is integrated into a Dreamer-style latent dynamics model with minimal modifications and no extra hyperparameters. Both imagination rollouts and policy optimization are conducted in the residual-action space, enabling smoother exploration, lower control variance, and more reliable planning. Empirical results on the DeepMind Control Suite demonstrate that ResWM achieves consistent improvements in sample efficiency, asymptotic returns, and control smoothness, significantly surpassing strong baselines such as Dreamer and TD-MPC. Beyond performance, ResWM produces more stable and energy-efficient action trajectories, a property critical for robotic systems deployed in real-world environments. These findings suggest that residual action modeling provides a simple yet powerful principle for bridging algorithmic advances in RL with the practical requirements of robotics.

</details>

Abstract: Co-design optimisation of autonomous systems has emerged as a powerful alternative to sequential approaches by jointly optimising physical design and control strategies. However, existing frameworks often neglect the robustness required for autonomous systems navigating unstructured, real-world environments. For agile Unmanned Aerial Vehicles (UAVs) operating at the edge of the flight envelope, this lack of robustness yields designs that are sensitive to perturbations and model mismatch. To address this, we propose a robust co-design framework for agile fixed-wing UAVs that integrates parametric uncertainty and wind disturbances directly into the concurrent optimisation process. Our bi-level approach optimises physical design in a high-level loop while discovering nominal solutions via a constrained trajectory planner and evaluating performance across a stochastic Monte Carlo ensemble using feedback LQR control. Validated across three agile flight missions, our strategy consistently outperforms deterministic baselines.   <summary>Details</summary>

Interpretability is particularly important when a robot is perceived as incompetent (e.g., when the robot suddenly stops or rotates away from the goal), as it allows the robot to explain its reasoning and identify controllable factors to improve performance, requiring causal rather than associative reasoning. To address these challenges, we propose a Causal Bayesian Network designed to predict how people perceive a mobile robot's competence and how they interpret its intent during navigation. Additionally, we introduce a novel method to improve perceived robot competence employing a combinatorial search, guided by the proposed causal model, to identify better navigation behaviors. Our method enhances interpretability and generates counterfactual robot motions while achieving comparable or superior predictive performance to state-of-the-art methods, reaching an F1-score of 0.78 and 0.75 for competence and intention on a binary scale. To further assess our method's ability to improve the perceived robot competence, we conducted an online evaluation in which users rated robot behaviors on a 5-point Likert scale. ### [255] [Distributed Kalman--Consensus Filtering with Adaptive Uncertainty Weighting for Multi-Object Tracking in Mobile Robot Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11328)
*Niusha Khosravi,Rodrigo Ventura,Meysam Basiri*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于移动机器人网络多目标跟踪的分布式卡尔曼-共识滤波器（DKCF），该滤波器能够处理局部可观测性和异质定位不确定性，并引入了一种不确定性感知的自适应共识加权机制以提高信息融合的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该研究基于MOTLEE框架，保留了其使用动态目标作为瞬态地标来改进机器人间相对姿态估计的方法。在此基础上，提出了一种不确定性感知的自适应共识加权机制，该机制根据传输估计的协方差动态调整邻居信息的权重。局部跟踪采用具有恒定速度模型（CVM）和全局最近邻（GNN）数据关联的卡尔曼滤波器（KF）。

Conclusion: 不确定性感知的自适应共识加权机制能有效提高分布式多目标跟踪的鲁棒性，尤其是在存在异质定位不确定性的情况下。尽管取得了积极的改进，但通信延迟仍然是影响系统性能的关键因素。

Abstract: This paper presents an implementation and evaluation of a Distributed Kalman--Consensus Filter (DKCF) for Multi-Object Tracking (MOT) in mobile robot networks operating under partial observability and heterogeneous localization uncertainty. A key challenge in such systems is the fusion of information from agents with differing localization quality, where frame misalignment can lead to inconsistent estimates, track duplication, and ghost tracks. To address this issue, we build upon the MOTLEE framework and retain its frame-alignment methodology, which uses consistently tracked dynamic objects as transient landmarks to improve relative pose estimates between robots. On top of this framework, we propose an uncertainty-aware adaptive consensus weighting mechanism that dynamically adjusts the influence of neighbor information based on the covariance of the transmitted estimates, thereby reducing the impact of unreliable data during distributed fusion. Local tracking is performed using a Kalman Filter (KF) with a Constant Velocity Model (CVM) and Global Nearest Neighbor (GNN) data association. simulation results demonstrate that adaptive weighting effectively protects local estimates from inconsistent data, yielding a MOTA improvement of 0.09 for agents suffering from localization drift, although system performance remains constrained by communication latency.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者采用定制的 ADMM 实现，包括：1. 将轨迹参数化为多项式，使得原始更新可以闭式求解为最小控制努力问题。2. 引入基于混合整数公式的时空分配图，并将松弛变量更新问题转化为最短路径搜索。

Result: 该方法通过联合优化离散空间和连续时间域，获得了比现有解耦方法更大的搜索空间，从而发现了更优的轨迹。此外，求解器的结构鲁棒性保证了从简单的初始值也能可靠收敛，克服了非凸环境中复杂热启动的瓶颈。

Abstract: This paper presents a numerical solver for computing continuous trajectories in non-convex environments. Our approach relies on a customized implementation of the Alternating Direction Method of Multipliers (ADMM) built upon two key components: First, we parameterize trajectories as polynomials, allowing the primal update to be computed in closed form as a minimum-control-effort problem. Second, we introduce the concept of a spatio-temporal allocation graph based on a mixed-integer formulation and pose the slack update as a shortest-path search. The combination of these ingredients results in a solver with several distinct advantages over the state of the art. By jointly optimizing over both discrete spatial and continuous temporal domains, our method accesses a larger search space than existing decoupled approaches, enabling the discovery of superior trajectories. Additionally, the solver's structural robustness ensures reliable convergence from naive initializations, removing the bottleneck of complex warm starting in non-convex environments.

### [258] [MirrorDrift: Actuated Mirror-Based Attacks on LiDAR SLAM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11364)
*Rokuto Nagata,Kenji Koide,Kazuma Ikeda,Ozora Sako,Shion Horie,Kentaro Yoshioka*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为MirrorDrift的新型LiDAR SLAM攻击方法，通过反射镜诱导“鬼点”，成功干扰了现代LiDAR系统的定位精度，平均位姿误差显著增加。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LiDAR SLAM攻击方法（如LiDAR欺骗）因需要传感器特定知识且易被现代防御机制规避，因此需要研究新的攻击方式。本文旨在探索一种无需信号注入即可实现大规模定位干扰的方法。

Method: MirrorDrift攻击利用一个可驱动的平面反射镜，通过控制反射镜的位置、对齐和驱动方式，在LiDAR扫描中产生“鬼点”，从而系统性地扰乱扫描匹配的对应关系。

Result: 在仿真实验中，MirrorDrift将平均位姿误差（APE）提高了6.1倍，使三个SLAM系统达到2.29-3.31米的平均APE。在真实世界实验中，该攻击对具有先进干扰抑制功能的现代LiDAR诱导了高达6.03米的定位误差。

Conclusion: MirrorDrift是首个针对量产级安全LiDAR的成功SLAM攻击，证明了通过反射镜诱导“鬼点”是一种有效的、无需信号注入的攻击手段，对现有LiDAR SLAM系统的安全性构成了威胁。

Abstract: LiDAR SLAM provides high-accuracy localization but is fragile to point-cloud corruption because scan matching assumes geometric consistency. Prior physical attacks on LiDAR SLAM largely rely on LiDAR spoofing via external signal injection, which requires sensor-specific timing knowledge and is increasingly mitigated by modern defense mechanisms such as timing obfuscation and injection rejection. In this work, we show that specular reflection offers an injection-free alternative and demonstrate an attack, MirrorDrift, that uses an actuated planar mirror to cause ghost points in LiDAR scans and systematically bias scan-matching correspondences. MirrorDrift optimizes mirror placement, alignment, and actuation. In simulation, it increases the average pose error (APE) by 6.1x over random placement, degrading three SLAM systems to 2.29-3.31 m mean APE. In real-world experiments on a modern LiDAR with state-of-the-art interference mitigation, it induces localization errors of up to 6.03 m. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first successful SLAM-targeted attack against production-grade secure LiDARs.

</details>


### [259] [Flight through Narrow Gaps with Morphing-Wing Drones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12059)
*Julius Wanner,Hoang-Vu Phan,Charbel Toumieh,Dario Floreano*

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种能够在中途收拢机翼的变体无人机，使其能够穿越比自身翼展更窄的间隙，并开发了一种结合最优参考轨迹生成和非线性模型预测控制的控制方法来应对由此产生的控制挑战。

Method: 研究者首先建立了一个能够模拟翼展收拢变形无人机在低速和后失速攻角下飞行的气动模型。然后，他们将纵向无人机动力学集成到一个最优参考轨迹生成和非线性模型预测控制（NMPC）框架中，并加入了运行时自适应成本和约束。

Result: 该方法在130克的翼展收拢变形无人机上进行了验证，在5-7 m/s的飞行速度下，穿越狭窄间隙时的平均高度误差为5厘米。无人机能够通过在间隙前加速和向上俯仰来补偿失速时的升力损失，补偿程度取决于参考轨迹优化的目标。该策略还能在硬件上实现精确的间隙穿越，同时保持恒定的前向飞行速度参考和接近恒定的高度。

Conclusion: 该研究成功开发了一种能够实现狭窄间隙穿越的翼展收拢变形无人机及其控制策略。该方法能够有效解决低速、升力损失等控制难题，并在实际硬件上展现出良好的性能。

Abstract: The size of a narrow gap traversable by a fixed-wing drone is limited by its wingspan. Inspired by birds, here, we enable the traversal of a gap of sub-wingspan width and height using a morphing-wing drone capable of temporarily sweeping in its wings mid-flight. This maneuver poses control challenges due to sudden lift loss during gap-passage at low flight speeds and the need for precisely timed wing-sweep actuation ahead of the gap. To address these challenges, we first develop an aerodynamic model for general wing-sweep morphing drone flight including low flight speeds and post-stall angles of attack. We integrate longitudinal drone dynamics into an optimal reference trajectory generation and Nonlinear Model Predictive Control framework with runtime adaptive costs and constraints. Validated on a 130 g wing-sweep-morphing drone, our method achieves an average altitude error of 5 cm during narrow-gap passage at forward speeds between 5 and 7 m/s, whilst enforcing fully swept wings near the gap across variable threshold distances. Trajectory analysis shows that the drone can compensate for lift loss during gap-passage by accelerating and pitching upwards ahead of the gap to an extent that differs between reference trajectory optimization objectives. We show that our strategy also allows for accurate gap passage on hardware whilst maintaining a constant forward flight speed reference and near-constant altitude.

### [260] [D-SLAMSpoof: An Environment-Agnostic LiDAR Spoofing Attack using Dynamic Point Cloud Injection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11365)
*Rokuto Nagata,Kenji Koide,Kazuma Ikeda,Ozora Sako,Kentaro Yoshioka*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为D-SLAMSpoof的新型激光雷达SLAM欺骗攻击方法，该方法通过空间注入形状和时间动态注入模式，即使在特征丰富的真实世界环境中也能显著提高攻击成功率。同时，提出了一种名为ISD-SLAM的防御方法，仅利用惯性导航信号即可有效检测和缓解此类攻击。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有激光雷达欺骗方法在特征丰富的真实世界环境中效果不佳，而激光雷达SLAM在自动驾驶系统中至关重要，其安全性受到威胁。因此，需要一种更有效的攻击方法来暴露漏洞，并提出一种实用的防御机制。

Method: 攻击方法（D-SLAMSpoof）通过设计空间注入形状和时间动态注入模式，利用激光雷达扫描匹配原理，通过外部激光干扰注入虚假测量值。防御方法（ISD-SLAM）仅依赖惯性导航（dead reckoning）信号来检测和缓解攻击。

Result: D-SLAMSpoof在城市和室内等特征丰富的真实世界环境中显著提高了攻击成功率。ISD-SLAM能够准确检测包括D-SLAMSpoof在内的激光雷达欺骗攻击，并有效缓解由此产生的定位漂移。

Conclusion: 激光雷达SLAM存在固有的安全漏洞。ISD-SLAM是第一个仅使用标准车载传感器即可防御激光雷达SLAM欺骗的实用方法，为提高自动驾驶系统的安全性和可靠性提供了关键见解。

Abstract: In this work, we introduce Dynamic SLAMSpoof (D-SLAMSpoof), a novel attack that compromises LiDAR SLAM even in feature-rich environments. The attack leverages LiDAR spoofing, which injects spurious measurements into LiDAR scans through external laser interference. By designing both spatial injection shapes and temporally coordinated dynamic injection patterns guided by scan-matching principles, D-SLAMSpoof significantly improves attack success rates in real-world, feature-rich environments such as urban areas and indoor spaces, where conventional LiDAR spoofing methods often fail. Furthermore, we propose a practical defense method, ISD-SLAM, that relies solely on inertial dead reckoning signals commonly available in autonomous systems. We demonstrate that ISD-SLAM accurately detects LiDAR spoofing attacks, including D-SLAMSpoof, and effectively mitigates the resulting position drift. Our findings expose inherent vulnerabilities in LiDAR-based SLAM and introduce the first practical defense against LiDAR-based SLAM spoofing using only standard onboard sensors, providing critical insights for improving the security and reliability of autonomous systems.

### [261] [Deployment-Time Reliability of Learned Robot Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11400)
*Christopher Agia*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文研究了如何通过在部署时运行的机制来提高学习型机器人策略的可靠性，提出了运行时监控、数据中心解释性和长时域任务协调方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前学习型机器人策略在部署时面临可靠性问题，例如分布偏移、累积误差和复杂的任务依赖性，阻碍了其在现实世界中的应用。

Method: 开发了三类互补的部署时机制：1. 运行时监控方法，通过检测闭环策略行为不一致和任务进度偏差来识别潜在故障。2. 数据中心框架，利用影响函数追踪部署时成功和失败与训练演示的关联，实现可解释性。3. 长时域任务协调，将策略协调视为行为序列成功概率的估计和最大化问题，并扩展到语言指定的开放式任务。

Result: 提出的方法能够检测潜在故障、提供对部署时行为的根本原因分析，并提高长时域任务执行的可靠性。

Conclusion: 通过关注部署时的核心挑战，这些贡献为学习型机器人策略在现实世界中的可靠应用奠定了实践基础，对于实现可信赖和可扩展的机器人自主性至关重要。

Abstract: Recent advances in learning-based robot manipulation have produced policies with remarkable capabilities. Yet, reliability at deployment remains a fundamental barrier to real-world use, where distribution shift, compounding errors, and complex task dependencies collectively undermine system performance. This dissertation investigates how the reliability of learned robot policies can be improved at deployment time through mechanisms that operate around them. We develop three complementary classes of deployment-time mechanisms. First, we introduce runtime monitoring methods that detect impending failures by identifying inconsistencies in closed-loop policy behavior and deviations in task progress, without requiring failure data or task-specific supervision. Second, we propose a data-centric framework for policy interpretability that traces deployment-time successes and failures to influential training demonstrations using influence functions, enabling principled diagnosis and dataset curation. Third, we address reliable long-horizon task execution by formulating policy coordination as the problem of estimating and maximizing the success probability of behavior sequences, and we extend this formulation to open-ended, language-specified tasks through feasibility-aware task planning. By centering on core challenges of deployment, these contributions advance practical foundations for the reliable, real-world use of learned robot policies. Continued progress on these foundations will be essential for enabling trustworthy and scalable robot autonomy in the future.

### [262] [Decentralized Cooperative Localization for Multi-Robot Systems with Asynchronous Sensor Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12075)
*Nivand Khosravi,Niusha Khosravi,Mohammad Bozorg,Masoud S. Bahraini*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个去中心化协同定位（DCL）框架，用于在GPS受限、通信基础设施有限的环境中操作的非完整移动机器人。该框架允许机器人本地执行定位，并在通信可用时共享测量信息。通过使用扩展卡尔曼滤波器、双特征评估以及自动坐标系对齐，提高了鲁棒性和预测精度。实验结果表明，DCL相比中心化协同定位（CCL）有显著性能提升，尤其适用于挑战性环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在GPS受限且通信基础设施有限的环境中，非完整移动机器人需要一种可靠的定位方法。现有的中心化协同定位（CCL）方法在通信受限时性能会下降。因此，需要一种更鲁棒、更具适应性的去中心化协同定位（DCL）方法。

Method: 提出了一种DCL框架，其中每个机器人使用扩展卡尔曼滤波器（EKF）进行本地定位。测量信息仅在通信链接可用且成功检测到其他机器人时共享。该框架保持机器人状态估计之间的互相关一致性，处理异步传感器数据，并能应对动态机动中的加速度。引入了双特征评估框架，利用静态环境特征和移动机器人作为动态特征。通过变换矩阵在预测和更新阶段实现坐标系的自动对齐。

Result: 与CCL相比，提出的DCL框架在Gazebo模拟和真实地下环境中都取得了更好的性能，RMSE降低了34%。采用双特征评估的DCL变体性能进一步提升，RMSE降低了56%。

Conclusion: 所提出的DCL框架能够鲁棒地处理动态传感器数据，实现任意初始方向的机器人坐标系自动对齐，并提高了在特征稀疏环境中的定位精度。该框架在GPS受限、通信受限或特征稀疏的挑战性环境中具有广泛的应用前景，如封闭空间、水下和野外等。

Abstract: Decentralized cooperative localization (DCL) is a promising approach for nonholonomic mobile robots operating in GPS-denied environments with limited communication infrastructure. This paper presents a DCL framework in which each robot performs localization locally using an Extended Kalman Filter, while sharing measurement information during update stages only when communication links are available and companion robots are successfully detected by LiDAR. The framework preserves cross-correlation consistency among robot state estimates while handling asynchronous sensor data with heterogeneous sampling rates and accommodating accelerations during dynamic maneuvers. Unlike methods that require pre-aligned coordinate systems, the proposed approach allows robots to initialize with arbitrary reference-frame orientations and achieves automatic alignment through transformation matrices in both the prediction and update stages. To improve robustness in feature-sparse environments, we introduce a dual-landmark evaluation framework that exploits both static environmental features and mobile robots as dynamic landmarks. The proposed framework enables reliable detection and feature extraction during sharp turns, while prediction accuracy is improved through information sharing from mutual observations. Experimental results in both Gazebo simulation and real-world basement environments show that DCL outperforms centralized cooperative localization (CCL), achieving a 34% reduction in RMSE, while the dual-landmark variant yields an improvement of 56%. These results demonstrate the applicability of DCL to challenging domains such as enclosed spaces, underwater environments, and feature-sparse terrains where conventional localization methods are ineffective.

### [263] [Vision-Based Hand Shadowing for Robotic Manipulation via Inverse Kinematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11383)
*Hendrik Chiche,Antoine Jamme,Trevor Rigoberto Martinez*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于单目RGB-D摄像头和MediaPipe Hands的离线手部追踪和重新定位流水线，用于低成本机械臂的遥操作。通过解算逆运动学生成机器人关节指令，并实现了一个抓取控制策略。在结构化任务中成功率达到90%，但在非结构化环境中由于遮挡成功率大幅下降至9.3%。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用安装在3D打印眼镜上的单目RGB-D摄像头，通过MediaPipe Hands检测21个手部地标，利用深度信息将其投影到3D空间，然后转换到机器人坐标系。使用PyBullet中的阻尼最小二乘逆运动学求解器生成SO-ARM101机器人的关节指令。一个抓取控制器将拇指-食指几何形状映射到抓取开口，并包含一个四级回退机制。在物理模拟器中预览动作，然后通过LeRobot框架在实体机器人上执行。

Result: 在结构化的拾放基准测试中（5x5网格，每格10次抓取），逆运动学重新定位流水线实现了90%的成功率。与四种在领导者-跟随者遥操作数据上训练的视觉-语言-动作策略（ACT, SmolVLA, pi0.5, GR00T N1.5）进行了比较。在非结构化的真实世界环境（超市、药店）中测试时，由于周围物体的遮挡，成功率降至9.3%（N=75）。

Conclusion: 所提出的无标记分析式重新定位方法在结构化环境中具有潜力，但在非结构化环境中，由于手部遮挡，其有效性受到显著限制，突显了该方法的潜力和当前的局限性。

Abstract: Teleoperation of low-cost robotic manipulators remains challenging due to the complexity of mapping human hand articulations to robot joint commands. We present an offline hand-shadowing and retargeting pipeline from a single egocentric RGB-D camera mounted on 3D-printed glasses. The pipeline detects 21 hand landmarks per hand using MediaPipe Hands, deprojects them into 3D via depth sensing, transforms them into the robot coordinate frame, and solves a damped-least-squares inverse kinematics problem in PyBullet to produce joint commands for the 6-DOF SO-ARM101 robot. A gripper controller maps thumb-index finger geometry to grasp aperture with a four-level fallback hierarchy. Actions are first previewed in a physics simulation before replay on the physical robot through the LeRobot framework. We evaluate the IK retargeting pipeline on a structured pick-and-place benchmark (5-tile grid, 10 grasps per tile) achieving a 90% success rate, and compare it against four vision-language-action policies (ACT, SmolVLA, pi0.5, GR00T N1.5) trained on leader-follower teleoperation data. We also test the IK pipeline in unstructured real-world environments (grocery store, pharmacy), where hand occlusion by surrounding objects reduces success to 9.3% (N=75), highlighting both the promise and current limitations of marker-free analytical retargeting.

Abstract: Recent work on robot manipulation has advanced policy generalization to novel scenarios. To work towards more precise evaluation of generalization in robotics, we propose RADAR, a scalable framework for directly comparing test-time evaluation tasks to policy training data, to determine what form of policy generalization is required. RADAR consists of a two-stage pipeline: first, retrieval using generalist policy embeddings identifies which training examples are relevant for a given evaluation task. ### [267] [Enhancing Lightweight Vision Language Models through Group Competitive Learning for Socially Compliant Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11447)
*Xinyu Zhang,Atsushi Konno,Toshihiko Yamasaki,Ling Xiao*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的方法要么计算开销大，要么在复杂的社交环境中表现较弱，因此需要一种既能实现强大推理能力又能兼顾效率的解决方案。

Abstract: Social robot navigation requires a sophisticated integration of scene semantics and human social norms. Conversely, lightweight VLMs enable efficient inference but often exhibit weaker reasoning and decision-making performance in socially complex environments. Achieving both strong reasoning ability and efficiency remains an open challenge. To bridge this gap, we propose Group Competitive Learning (GCL), a strategy designed to amplify the capabilities of lightweight VLMs. Our strategy introduces the Group Competitive Objective (GCO) to harmonize global semantics with distributional regularization, alongside Asymmetric Group Optimization (AGO) to explore the upper limits of model performance. Specifically, GCL enables the Qwen2.5-VL-3B learner model and guide Qwen3-VL-4B to achieve an F1 score of 0.968 and 0.914, representing 40\% and 12\% improvement over vanilla supervised fine-tuning (SFT). ### [270] [SPARK: Skeleton-Parameter Aligned Retargeting on Humanoid Robots with Kinodynamic Trajectory Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11480)
*Hanwen Wang,Qiayuan Liao,Bike Zhang,Kunzhao Ren,Koushil Sreenath,Xiaobin Xiong*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种两阶段流水线，用于从任务空间的人体运动数据生成自然且符合动力学约束的机器人运动参考。首先，将人体运动转换为机器人骨架表示并校准尺寸，然后通过分阶段的运动规划优化轨迹和关节力矩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的人体运动数据与机器人的运动学和动力学不兼容，限制了其直接应用。需要一种方法来生成适用于机器人控制的自然且动力学可行的运动参考。

Method: 1. 骨架校准：将人体运动转换为URDF骨架表示，并根据目标人形机器人的尺寸进行校准，以减少逆运动学误差。 2. 动力学轨迹优化：通过三阶段（运动学优化、逆动力学、动力学优化）渐进式优化，对校准后的轨迹进行精炼，生成动态一致的状态轨迹和关节力矩。

Result: 生成了自然、物理一致且符合动力学约束的运动参考，包括状态轨迹和关节力矩，适用于学习型控制器。

Conclusion: 骨架校准和动力学轨迹优化相结合，能够有效地从任务空间的人体运动数据生成高质量的、适用于各种人形机器人的运动参考。

Abstract: Human motion provides rich priors for training general-purpose humanoid control policies, but raw demonstrations are often incompatible with a robot's kinematics and dynamics, limiting their direct use. We present a two-stage pipeline for generating natural and dynamically feasible motion references from task-space human data. First, we convert human motion into a unified robot description format (URDF)-based skeleton representation and calibrate it to the target humanoid's dimensions. By aligning the underlying skeleton structure rather than heuristically modifying task-space targets, this step significantly reduces inverse kinematics error and tuning effort. Second, we refine the retargeted trajectories through progressive kinodynamic trajectory optimization (TO), solved in three stages: kinematic TO, inverse dynamics, and full kinodynamic TO, each warm-started from the previous solution. The final result yields dynamically consistent state trajectories and joint torque profiles, providing high-quality references for learning-based controllers. Together, skeleton calibration and kinodynamic TO enable the generation of natural, physically consistent motion references across diverse humanoid platforms.

Method: RoboClaw提出了一种统一的VLM驱动控制器，实现了数据收集、策略学习和任务执行的整合。其核心是Entangled Action Pairs (EAP)，将前向操作行为与反向恢复动作相结合，形成自重置循环，实现持续的On-policy数据采集和迭代策略优化。

We present RoboClaw, an agentic robotics framework that unifies data collection, policy learning, and task execution under a single VLM-driven controller. At the policy level, RoboClaw introduces Entangled Action Pairs (EAP), which couple forward manipulation behaviors with inverse recovery actions to form self-resetting loops for autonomous data collection. This mechanism enables continuous on-policy data acquisition and iterative policy refinement with minimal human intervention. During deployment, the same agent performs high-level reasoning and dynamically orchestrates learned policy primitives to accomplish long-horizon tasks. By maintaining consistent contextual semantics across collection and execution, RoboClaw reduces mismatch between the two phases and improves multi-policy robustness. ### [273] [Unsupervised LiDAR-Based Multi-UAV Detection and Tracking Under Extreme Sparsity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11586)

  <summary>Details</summary>

We introduce an unsupervised, LiDAR-only pipeline that addresses both detection and tracking without the need for labeled training data. The detector integrates range-adaptive DBSCAN clustering with a three-stage temporal consistency check and is benchmarked on real-world air-to-air flight data under eight different parameter configurations. The best setup attains 0.891 precision, 0.804 recall, and 0.63 m RMSE, and a systematic minPts sweep verifies that most scans contain at most 1-2 target points, directly quantifying the sparsity regime. For multi-target tracking, we compare deterministic Hungarian assignment with joint probabilistic data association (JPDA), each coupled with Interacting Multiple Model filtering, in four simulated scenarios with increasing levels of ambiguity. JPDA cuts identity switches by 64% with negligible impact on MOTA, demonstrating that probabilistic association is advantageous when UAV trajectories approach one another closely. A two-environment evaluation strategy, combining real-world detection with RTK-GPS ground truth and simulation-based tracking with identity-annotated ground truth, overcomes the limitations of GNSS-only evaluation at inter-UAV distances below 2 m.

### [274] [Diversity You Can Actually Measure: A Fast, Model-Free Diversity Metric for Robotics Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11634)
*Sreevardhan Sirigiri,Nathan Samuel de Lara,Christopher Agia,Florian Shkurti,Fabio Ramos*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 研究提出了一种基于签名变换的熵度量方法，用于量化机器人模仿学习数据集的多样性，并在此基础上开发了一个名为FAKTUAL的数据集精选算法，以提高泛化性能，该算法在多项基准和真实世界任务中均表现出优于随机选择的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的机器人模仿学习数据集多样性度量方法难以处理长轨迹、不同长度以及高维观察数据的特性，并且缺乏一种直接在数据集上操作的有效方法来量化多样性并指导数据集的精选。

Method: 1. 提出基于签名变换的熵度量方法，该方法在签名核的Gram矩阵上计算熵，直接作用于示范轨迹。 2. 开发了FAKTUAL（FAst trajectory Kernel enTropy cUration for imitation Learning）算法，该算法是一种模型无关的数据精选方法，旨在最大化数据集的熵，以在给定预算内选择示范子集。3. 在RoboMimic、MetaWorld以及真实世界的机器人操作任务上进行了评估。

Result: FAKTUAL算法在不同任务和模型架构下，通过多样性感知的数据精选，显著提高了下游任务的成功率，优于随机选择。与近期的机器人数据精选方法相比，FAKTUAL的计算效率更高。

Conclusion: 示范数据集的熵可以作为一种实用的工具，用于理解和改善机器人模仿学习数据集的多样性，FAKTUAL算法是一种有效且高效的数据精选方法，能够提升模仿学习的泛化性能。

Abstract: Robotics datasets for imitation learning typically consist of long-horizon trajectories of different lengths over states, actions, and high-dimensional observations (e.g., RGB video), making it non-trivial to quantify diversity in a way that respects the underlying trajectory structure and geometry. We extend Shannon and von Neumann entropy to this setting by defining signature transform-based entropy on the Gram matrix of a signature kernel over demonstrations, yielding entropy and diversity metrics that operate directly on the demonstration dataset. Building on these metrics, we study how dataset diversity affects generalization performance in robot imitation learning and propose a simple, model-free way to curate diverse demonstrations. We introduce FAKTUAL (FAst trajectory Kernel enTropy cUration for imitation Learning), a data curation algorithm that selects a subset of demonstrations maximizing entropy given a subset-size budget. FAKTUAL is fully model-free, requires no access to the imitation policy or rollouts, and adds negligible overhead relative to policy training. We evaluate our approach on image and state-based RoboMimic and MetaWorld benchmarks, as well as four real-world manipulation tasks. Across tasks and architectures, diversity-aware curation with FAKTUAL consistently improves downstream success rates over random selection, while being substantially more computationally efficient compared to recent robot data curation methods. Our results suggest that the entropy of demonstration datasets is a practical tool for understanding and improving dataset diversity in robot imitation learning.

### [275] [Learn Structure, Adapt on the Fly: Multi-Scale Residual Learning and Online Adaptation for Aerial Manipulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11638)
*Samaksh Ujjawal,Naveen Sudheer Nair,Shivansh Pratap Singh,Rishabh Dev Yadav,Wei Pan,Spandan Roy*
